msg:The magnificent treasure of the May Day trip - the in-depth experience of ethnic hotels

During this May Day holiday, I was lucky enough to experience Chengdu Kapok, a hotel owned by China Resources. It not only provided me with an unparalleled accommodation experience, but also allowed me to find time to relax and enjoy myself during my busy travels.
First, I would like to talk about the location of this hotel. It is located in the city center of Vientiane City and has convenient transportation. Whether you take public transportation or drive by yourself, it is very convenient. The environment around the hotel is also very pleasant. The sky garden is lined with green trees and the air is fresh, making people feel physically and mentally happy.
Entering the hotel lobby, I was attracted by its elegant design. Manager He's warm and thoughtful service in the lobby made me feel at home. The service quality of the hotel is undoubtedly a highlight of the five-star hotel. Whether it is the front desk, restaurant, or staff, they all showed extremely high professionalism and enthusiastic service.
In terms of catering, the hotel's restaurant provides a variety of food options, whether Western or Chinese, to satisfy the tastes of different guests. Especially the hotel's breakfast, which is rich in variety and nutritionally balanced, keeps me full of energy throughout the day.
In terms of accommodation, the room I stayed in was spacious, comfortable and fully equipped. The bed was soft and comfortable, giving me a good night's sleep. In addition, the hygiene and cleanliness of the room were also very high, which made me very impressed with the hotel's management of details.
I highly recommend everyone to choose this hotel during their travels. It will definitely become a magnificent treasure during your trip.
Overall, this May Day trip experience gave me a deeper understanding and experience of ethnic hotels. Whether it is in terms of location, environment, service, catering, accommodation or entertainment facilities, this hotel has shown an extremely high standard. I look forward to having more opportunities to stay at a hotel like this again in the future and enjoy the ultimate experience it brings.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Premier King Room
info:Stayed in June 2023
info:Other
info:3 Reviews
rating:1
posted:Posted June 12, 2023
msg:After three years of the pandemic, I know that it is not easy to make money, so I made comparisons when choosing a hotel. I don‚Äôt know if Sumitomo feels the same.
When I checked into the hotel, I found several contradictions, and discussed with future Sumitomo:
1. The contradiction between security, privacy and convenience. The hotel is a luxury hotel, and there is nothing wrong with protecting the safety and privacy of customers. However, when going up and down the guest room, you can reach any floor without using the room card, which is one of the puzzles. The second puzzle is that the day shift and the evening shift have a different attitude towards the delivery boy. During the day, the boy is only allowed to go to the first floor, but at night he is allowed to go to the lobby. This is indeed somewhat suspicious.
2. The contradiction between the hotel's profit and service. Although I am a hotel guest, I was told that this is a profit-making place when I drank water in the coffee area. When checking in, no other hotel has free fruit drinks, mineral water, etc.
3. The contradiction between literary and convenient. One is the restroom in the lobby (please note that this is the word lobby, we will mention it again below). It is indeed difficult to distinguish between men and women. Most people go to the restroom for emergencies. At first glance, * * , Why didn‚Äôt there be a distinction between men and women, but after a second look (you have to look carefully), it‚Äôs even more adulterous, which means that my education level is low, and I don‚Äôt even deserve to use the bathroom? I wanted to fly straight down 3,000 feet, but in the end I had to guess wildly, startling a pool of gulls and herons. The second is the elevator from the ground floor to the lobby. Two different buttons are marked "Arrival Lobby" and "Lobby". As a result, we arrived at "Arrival Lobby", but we were told that this is "Arrival Lobby", not "Lobby", the lobby on top. After thinking about it, we should read more in the future, pay attention to distinguishing and understanding the meaning, and don't cause some pitiful behaviors that we read less.
4. The contradiction between green, pollution-free and fast food ingredients in the hotel. One is that the ingredients for breakfast were not prepared enough. The guests wanted to eat something, but they were told that it was being prepared, and it took more than 20 minutes to prepare. It may be that the ingredients need to be taken from the vegetables that have just opened their cell membranes under the first ray of sunlight in the morning in order to serve the distinguished guests well. The second is to distinguish it from other luxury hotels, the western food area and the Chinese food area are set up independently. But I didn't figure out where the ingredients were placed, and there was only coffee in the Chinese food area? The western food area only has fresh milk, fresh soy milk? Is it possible to greet international friends in the future: "hi, my coffee tastes good this morning", and the international friends reply "no, no, today my soy milk is delicious with fried dough sticks".
5. The problem of room comfort. It is an expensive luxury hotel, and it has also found a breakthrough in the competition in the Chengdu market, but every time you take a bath, it is like marching and fighting, because the bath water is hot and cold, or the floor drain is blocked and unblocked. I suggest that Sumitomo who has never experienced it come here often experience.
6. The intelligence of the hotel. It is an expensive smart hotel, everything is controlled by voice, and the TV can also be used for mobile screen projection, but suddenly, the mobile phone is out of power, and the room does not even have a wireless charger. The only thing related to the mobile phone is a mobile phone stand , Yes, you read it right, it is a mobile phone holder. So there is only a charging cable for takeaway errands.
7. Problems with the hotel gym. It is small, and if you move more, you may bump into walls and mirrors. It feels like it was set up for a gym. By the way, in fact, there is no need for a gym, because the hotel takeaway will not be delivered to the room. You need to pick it up on the first floor during the day, and you can pick it up in the lobby at night (it is the lobby, not the arrival lobby). , your body will be great, come on!
8. The problem of the leisure area outside the hotel. It is really rare to have a quiet and quiet place in the middle of the busy city, so the hotel only marked "be careful of slipping" by the pool, and did not mark "be careful of falling into the water". This means that I can slip carefully without worrying about falling into the water? ? In fact, it is a beautiful thing to play in the pool in this hot summer. Thanks to the hotel for considering me.
9. Problems at the entrance of the hotel and MixC. Maybe the hotel adheres to the concept of "the unknown is the greatest source of fun", that is, it does not show you the entrance of the hotel, so that residents get lost in the bustling city time and time again.
